<Date>1558908207693< /Date>< rate>
5< /rate>
<Text>Cudahy is one of the most quirky and hidden small towns I've visited. That's a compliment! It's funny, I've been in this community dozens of times throughout my life over the years. But I've visited the library, or let alone the park, until month ago. Yet again, I've discovered some unique gems that adds a special charm to any community. This park is smaller in contrast to Salt Lake Park or Furman Park. However, this site is nearby the L.A. River, a few American Craftsman homes, an elementary school, City Hall and Public Library. Additionally, there's a small skatepark, basketball court, River Bike Pathway, Baseball Field, and Children's Play Section. Overall, it's a decent park and at night, you're able to view the Schutlz Steel Factory from afar and the cars passing to Bell from the bridge.</Text>< Pictures>
None</Pictures>

<text>So the way this place works is, you grab a package or two of meat (lots of choices) and fill a salad bowl with veggies from the veggie bar (about 24 choices). Then you choose seasonings (14 choices) and up to 6 sauces (lemon, garlic, oyster, Mongolian, mild spicy, spicy). They add noodles and grill it for you in about two minutes. It's similar quality, taste and price to standard Asian buffet fare, but you have custom control over the ingredients and flavorings. You just don't get the unlimited portions aspect. Still was a lot of food for $14. Essentially two meals.</text><rating>5<//rating><name>David Y.</name><pictures>[{'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipOz56RrV5YQ-iqu8Y-RjB_Csjfw2QN10xMvGA-w=w150-h150-k-no-p']}]<//pictures>< Date>

< Text>
This was a great experience for us! We were greeted by the cooks and the lady at the register. I explained that we were new and asked how to order two pack meat BBQ. She was pleasant and friendly showed us the freezers and told us to pick any two meats and the vegetables plus the sauces. We handed them to the cooks who stir fried them right in front of us on the large grill. The aroma made us so hungry lol and the food was ready in a few minutes üëç you can choose between rice or noodles and a huge selection of vegetables were available.  The place isn't large but good enough seating for about 30 people and in the middle of a large area surrounded by restaurants. We will be back for the spicy pork bento I heard its really good! Oh BTW the food we ate was so delicious üç≤üëç</Text>

Also they give you a small little bowl in which you compile your ingredients to make your dish. I used 2 bowls and they tried to charge another $5. A ripoff if you ask me. They portion noodles for you if you want them.. they have rice available at no extra charge, but it's not posted anywhere and is nowhere's to be seen in the place. < Review>
Interesting place. It's more Cafe style than table service. You order at the counter or start your bbq plate and pay at the cashier.  sign says Mongolian bbq but there are also sushi rolls, Japanese bento, and Korean bibimbap on the menu. The meat for the BBQ is pre-portioned into boxes and you pay by how many boxes you want so no overstuffed meat bowls here. I would say that this is more sanitary than having everyone go at the same tray of meat all night. Veggies and sauces are standard and there is a spice tray as well if you want to add some oregano or cumin. The most interesting thing on the menu is Korean ramen. Like the packaged kind. There's several brands available and several varieties of toppings too. I'll have to try that next time and relive my college days.<//Review>

< text>
The Habit occupies a happy place in between fast food and the $15 and up hamburger that you would get at a sit down restaurant. For sides, fries are tasty, the onion rings are delicious (ordering half fries and half rings is my personal favorite), and the tempora green beans are excellent. They also have a variety of salads if you are looking for something on the lighter side.  This particular location has lots of parking nearby and it's pretty easy to get in and out. If you come at lunch or dinner time, you should expect a little bit of a wait as this is a popular location.< /text>

<Name>Jasmine Johnson</Name><Response>None< /Response>< review>
This restaurant located off of La Cumbre Rd. Also can access through the La Cumbre shopping center entrances from State St.
They serve all the Hamburger Habit selections of burgers, chicken sandwiches, salads, shakes, sides and kids meals. This restaurant in Santa Barbara also serves turkey burgers. Excellent preparation of food ordered.
Table / booth seating inside and outdoor patio seating also.
Has soda, lemonade, ice tea and water dispensers, along with their condiments, ketchup, jalepenos, yellow peppers and peperoccini's.
Expedient and friendly in their service during order and pick up of the entrees ordered.
Clean facility and restroom for patrons of restaurant.
Parking limited in front of location,  but can park nearby and use shopping center spaces also.</review>

< Rating>
4</Rating>
< Text>
There's always a long line here and when it's slightly warm outside, it's uncomfortably hot in here!!! However, the food makes up for it. I love their Chile Verde and their Quesadilla is huge and delicious. Everything here is great. You get in line and look through the glass and order what you want. They prepare it and you wait for it. It's not as quick as you'd think but I don't mind waiting since you can munch on a variety of salsas while you sit and wait for them to bring you your food. They've won awards for their awesome salsas and I do think they are all very good. They have a few fresh juices to choose from as well. When I want hot, fresh and cheap authentic Mexican food, I go to Pancho Villa! I've even jumped off Bart on my way home just to have a quick bite.</Text>

< review>
Habit Burger: Make it a Family Night & Healthier Habit when it comes to fast & casual dining. My family loves to take our multi-generation group to this Habit Burger. We used to go to the one on El Camino (Sunnyvale) but ever since this new location in Cupertino opened on Steven‚Äôs Creek we have been dining at this location more frequently. Not only is this location newer and clean, the indoor seating is more spacious and has more booths to sit in (ideal for my Grandpa) especially when we need the AC for very hot days and the heater for the colder nights. My favorite to order is the Santa Barbara Salad (for the hotter weather) with no cheese and dressing on the side. I have a severe dairy allergy and the restaurant is always very careful about accommodating it. They even put an allergy tag on the item that contains the allergy dish. I also like the Santa Barbara burger (it has avocado yum) and they make it for me on the Sourdough with no butter, no mayo, and no cheese. I have even had a few cashiers inform me when we were ordering that they could do this for me (they are knowledgeable about food allergy specifics and preparation), pleasant about the food allergy specifics, and genuinely helpful. My family loves the Santa Barbara burger. Sometimes they will switch it up with a regular burger or Cesar Salad. We usually get the Sweet Potato fries on the side (not too mushy or crispy, just right) and onion rings for my Grandpa. Highly recommend for families or groups of people that have a dairy sensitive or dairy allergy in the group, just make sure you inform your cashier of the allergy when ordering.<//review>
